[30;1m41 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35mHTTPretty is a python library that swaps the modules :py:mod:`socket`[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35mand :py:mod:`ssl` with fake implementations that intercept HTTP[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35mrequests at the level of a TCP connection.[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35mIt is inspired on Ruby's `FakeWeb <http://fakeweb.rubyforge.org/>`_.[0m
[30;1m47 | [0m[35m[0m
